               <td class="crayon-code">
                <div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 11px !important; line-height: 16px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;">
                 <div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-59beb9e590435350906779-1">
                  <span class="crayon-sy">(</span>
                  <span class="crayon-sy">?</span>
                  <span class="crayon-o">:</span>
                  <span class="crayon-sy">[</span>
                  <span class="crayon-v">a</span>
                  <span class="crayon-o">-</span>
                  <span class="crayon-v">z0</span>
                  <span class="crayon-o">-</span>
                  <span class="crayon-cn">9</span>
                  <span class="crayon-o">!</span>
                  <span class="crayon-p">#$%&amp;'*+/=?^_`{|}~-]+(?:\.[a-z0-9!#$%&amp;'*+/=?^_`{|}~-]+)*|"(?:[\x01-\x08\x0b\x0c\x0e-\x1f\x21\x23-\x5b\x5d-\x7f]|\\[\x01-\x09\x0b\x0c\x0e-\x7f])*")@(?:(?:[a-z0-9](?:[a-z0-9-]*[a-z0-9])?\.)+[a-z0-9](?:[a-z0-9-]*[a-z0-9])?|\[(?:(?:25[0-5]|2[0-4][0-9]|[01]?[0-9][0-9]?)\.){3}(?:25[0-5]|2[0-4][0-9]|[01]?[0-9][0-9]?|[a-z0-9-]*[a-z0-9]:(?:[\x01-\x08\x0b\x0c\x0e-\x1f\x21-\x5a\x53-\x7f]|\\[\x01-\x09\x0b\x0c\x0e-\x7f])+)\])</span>

          <p>In case you ever wonder, below is the&nbsp;regex used in&nbsp;type=email from&nbsp;<a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/html-markup/input.email.html#input.email.attrs.value.multiple">W3C</a>:</p> 
          <div class="datatype-desc"> 
           <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
           <div id="crayon-59beb9e59044a374474619" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-prism-like crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-always wrap" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 11px !important; line-height: 16px !important;"> 
            <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 11px !important;height: 16.5px !important; line-height: 16.5px !important;">

func validateEmail(candidate: String) -&gt; Bool {
 let emailRegex = "[A-Z0-9a-z._%+-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.-]+\\.[A-Za-z]{2,64}"
 return NSPredicate(format: "SELF MATCHES %@", emailRegex).evaluateWithObject(candidate)
}</textarea>

           <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
            <textarea class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 11px !important; line-height: 16px !important;">
Function isEmail(ByVal email as string) as boolean
    Static emailRegex As New Regex("^[_a-z0-9-]+(.[a-z0-9-]+)@[a-z0-9-]+(.[a-z0-9-]+)*(.[a-z]{2,4})$")

    return emailRegex.IsMatch(email)
End Function</textarea>
           </div>

          <h2>Find All Email Addresses in a File using Grep</h2> 
          <p></p>
          <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
          <div id="crayon-59beb9e59048a076266890" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-prism-like crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-always wrap" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 11px !important; line-height: 16px !important;"> 
           <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 11px !important;height: 16.5px !important; line-height: 16.5px !important;">

          <h2>SQL Server Email Validation</h2> 
          <p></p>
          <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
          <div id="crayon-59beb9e59048d415696964" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-prism-like crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-always wrap" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 11px !important; line-height: 16px !important;"> 
           <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 11px !important;height: 16.5px !important; line-height: 16.5px !important;">
            <span class="crayon-title"></span> 
            <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 11px !important;height: 16.5px !important; line-height: 16.5px !important;">
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div> 
           <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 15.4px !important; line-height: 15.4px !important;"></div> 
           <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
            <textarea class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 11px !important; line-height: 16px !important;">
 select email 
 from table_name where 
 patindex ('%[ &amp;'',":;!+=\/()&lt;&gt;]%', email) &gt; 0 -- Invalid characters
 or patindex ('[@.-_]%', email) &gt; 0 -- Valid but cannot be starting character
 or patindex ('%[@.-_]', email) &gt; 0 -- Valid but cannot be ending character
 or email not like '%@%.%' -- Must contain at least one @ and one .
 or email like '%..%' -- Cannot have two periods in a row
 or email like '%@%@%' -- Cannot have two @ anywhere
 or email like '%.@%' or email like '%@.%' -- Cannot have @ and . next to each other
 or email like '%.cm' or email like '%.co' -- Camaroon or Colombia? Typos. 
 or email like '%.or' or email like '%.ne' -- Missing last letter</textarea>
           </div>

          <h2>Oracle PL/SQL Email Regex</h2> 
          <p></p>
          <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
          <div id="crayon-59beb9e59048f543595192" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-prism-like crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-always wrap" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 11px !important; line-height: 16px !important;"> 
           <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 11px !important;height: 16.5px !important; line-height: 16.5px !important;">
            <span class="crayon-title"></span>

            <textarea class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 11px !important; line-height: 16px !important;">
SELECT email 
FROM table_name
WHERE REGEXP_LIKE (email, '[A-Z0-9._%-]+@[A-Z0-9._%-]+\.[A-Z]{2,4}');</textarea>

                  2
                 </div>

                  3
                 </div>
                </div> </td> 
               <td class="crayon-code">
                <div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 11px !important; line-height: 16px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;">
                 <div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-59beb9e59048f543595192-1">
                  <span class="crayon-e">SELECT </span>
                  <span class="crayon-e">email </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-59beb9e59048f543595192-2">
                  <span class="crayon-e">FROM </span>
                  <span class="crayon-e">table_name</span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-59beb9e59048f543595192-3">
                  <span class="crayon-e">WHERE </span>
                  <span class="crayon-e">REGEXP_LIKE</span>
                  <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                  <span class="crayon-sy">(</span>
                  <span class="crayon-v">email</span>
                  <span class="crayon-sy">,</span>
                  <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                  <span class="crayon-s">'[A-Z0-9._%-]+@[A-Z0-9._%-]+\.[A-Z]{2,4}'</span>
                  <span class="crayon-sy">)</span>
                  <span class="crayon-sy">;</span>
                 </div>
                </div></td> 
              </tr>
